simulator = 'verilator', timescale = '1ps/1ps'
tbpath = '/workspaces/lab-4-behavioral-verilog-jasonwaseq/part2/regdelaybuffer'
params = {'delay_p': 4, 'width_p': 7}, defs = [], testname = 'single_test'
pymodule = 'test_regdelaybuffer'
jsonpath = '/workspaces/lab-4-behavioral-verilog-jasonwaseq/part2/regdelaybuffer'
jsonname = 'filelist.json'
root = '/workspaces/lab-4-behavioral-verilog-jasonwaseq'

    def runner(simulator, timescale, tbpath, params, defs=[], testname=None, pymodule=None, jsonpath=None, jsonname="filelist.json", root=None):
        """Run the simulator on test n, with parameters params, and defines
        defs. If n is none, it will run all tests"""
    
        # if json path is none, assume that it is the same as tbpath
        if(jsonpath is None):
            jsonpath = tbpath
    
        assert (os.path.exists(jsonpath)), "jsonpath directory must exist"
        top = get_top(jsonpath, jsonname)
    
        # if pymodule is none, assume that the python module name is test+<name of the top module>.
        if(pymodule is None):
            pymodule = "test_" + top
    
        if(testname is None):
            testdir = "all"
        else:
            testdir=testname
    
        # Assume all paths in the json file are relative to the repository root.
        if(root is None):
            root = git.Repo(search_parent_directories=True).working_tree_dir
    
        assert (os.path.exists(root)), "root directory path must exist"
    
        sources = get_sources(root, tbpath)
    
        work_dir = os.path.join(tbpath, "run", testdir, get_param_string(params), simulator)
        build_dir = os.path.join(tbpath, "build", get_param_string(params))
    
        # Icarus doesn't build, it just runs.
        if simulator.startswith("icarus"):
            build_dir = work_dir
    
        if simulator.startswith("verilator"):
            compile_args=["-Wno-fatal", "-DVM_TRACE_FST=1", "-DVM_TRACE=1"]
            plus_args = ["--trace", "--trace-fst"]
            if(not os.path.exists(work_dir)):
                os.makedirs(work_dir)
        else:
            compile_args=[]
            plus_args = []
    
>       run(verilog_sources=sources,
            simulator=simulator,
            toplevel=top,
            module=pymodule,
            compile_args=compile_args,
            plus_args=plus_args,
            sim_build=build_dir,
            timescale=timescale,
            parameters=params,
            defines=defs + ["VM_TRACE_FST=1", "VM_TRACE=1"],
            work_dir=work_dir,
            waves=True,
            testcase=testname)

simulator = 'verilator', timescale = '1ps/1ps'
tbpath = '/workspaces/lab-4-behavioral-verilog-jasonwaseq/part2/regdelaybuffer'
params = {'delay_p': 2, 'width_p': 32}, defs = [], testname = 'single_test'
pymodule = 'test_regdelaybuffer'
jsonpath = '/workspaces/lab-4-behavioral-verilog-jasonwaseq/part2/regdelaybuffer'
jsonname = 'filelist.json'
root = '/workspaces/lab-4-behavioral-verilog-jasonwaseq'

    def runner(simulator, timescale, tbpath, params, defs=[], testname=None, pymodule=None, jsonpath=None, jsonname="filelist.json", root=None):
        """Run the simulator on test n, with parameters params, and defines
        defs. If n is none, it will run all tests"""
    
        # if json path is none, assume that it is the same as tbpath
        if(jsonpath is None):
            jsonpath = tbpath
    
        assert (os.path.exists(jsonpath)), "jsonpath directory must exist"
        top = get_top(jsonpath, jsonname)
    
        # if pymodule is none, assume that the python module name is test+<name of the top module>.
        if(pymodule is None):
            pymodule = "test_" + top
    
        if(testname is None):
            testdir = "all"
        else:
            testdir=testname
    
        # Assume all paths in the json file are relative to the repository root.
        if(root is None):
            root = git.Repo(search_parent_directories=True).working_tree_dir
    
        assert (os.path.exists(root)), "root directory path must exist"
    
        sources = get_sources(root, tbpath)
    
        work_dir = os.path.join(tbpath, "run", testdir, get_param_string(params), simulator)
        build_dir = os.path.join(tbpath, "build", get_param_string(params))
    
        # Icarus doesn't build, it just runs.
        if simulator.startswith("icarus"):
            build_dir = work_dir
    
        if simulator.startswith("verilator"):
            compile_args=["-Wno-fatal", "-DVM_TRACE_FST=1", "-DVM_TRACE=1"]
            plus_args = ["--trace", "--trace-fst"]
            if(not os.path.exists(work_dir)):
                os.makedirs(work_dir)
        else:
            compile_args=[]
            plus_args = []
    
>       run(verilog_sources=sources,
            simulator=simulator,
            toplevel=top,
            module=pymodule,
            compile_args=compile_args,
            plus_args=plus_args,
            sim_build=build_dir,
            timescale=timescale,
            parameters=params,
            defines=defs + ["VM_TRACE_FST=1", "VM_TRACE=1"],
            work_dir=work_dir,
            waves=True,
            testcase=testname)

simulator = 'verilator', timescale = '1ps/1ps'
tbpath = '/workspaces/lab-4-behavioral-verilog-jasonwaseq/part2/regdelaybuffer'
params = {'delay_p': 2, 'width_p': 7}, defs = [], testname = 'inout_fuzz_test'
pymodule = 'test_regdelaybuffer'
jsonpath = '/workspaces/lab-4-behavioral-verilog-jasonwaseq/part2/regdelaybuffer'
jsonname = 'filelist.json'
root = '/workspaces/lab-4-behavioral-verilog-jasonwaseq'

    def runner(simulator, timescale, tbpath, params, defs=[], testname=None, pymodule=None, jsonpath=None, jsonname="filelist.json", root=None):
        """Run the simulator on test n, with parameters params, and defines
        defs. If n is none, it will run all tests"""
    
        # if json path is none, assume that it is the same as tbpath
        if(jsonpath is None):
            jsonpath = tbpath
    
        assert (os.path.exists(jsonpath)), "jsonpath directory must exist"
        top = get_top(jsonpath, jsonname)
    
        # if pymodule is none, assume that the python module name is test+<name of the top module>.
        if(pymodule is None):
            pymodule = "test_" + top
    
        if(testname is None):
            testdir = "all"
        else:
            testdir=testname
    
        # Assume all paths in the json file are relative to the repository root.
        if(root is None):
            root = git.Repo(search_parent_directories=True).working_tree_dir
    
        assert (os.path.exists(root)), "root directory path must exist"
    
        sources = get_sources(root, tbpath)
    
        work_dir = os.path.join(tbpath, "run", testdir, get_param_string(params), simulator)
        build_dir = os.path.join(tbpath, "build", get_param_string(params))
    
        # Icarus doesn't build, it just runs.
        if simulator.startswith("icarus"):
            build_dir = work_dir
    
        if simulator.startswith("verilator"):
            compile_args=["-Wno-fatal", "-DVM_TRACE_FST=1", "-DVM_TRACE=1"]
            plus_args = ["--trace", "--trace-fst"]
            if(not os.path.exists(work_dir)):
                os.makedirs(work_dir)
        else:
            compile_args=[]
            plus_args = []
    
>       run(verilog_sources=sources,
            simulator=simulator,
            toplevel=top,
            module=pymodule,
            compile_args=compile_args,
            plus_args=plus_args,
            sim_build=build_dir,
            timescale=timescale,
            parameters=params,
            defines=defs + ["VM_TRACE_FST=1", "VM_TRACE=1"],
            work_dir=work_dir,
            waves=True,
            testcase=testname)
E       SystemExit: FAILED 1 tests.

simulator = 'verilator', timescale = '1ps/1ps'
tbpath = '/workspaces/lab-4-behavioral-verilog-jasonwaseq/part2/regdelaybuffer'
params = {'delay_p': 4, 'width_p': 32}, defs = [], testname = 'in_fuzz_test'
pymodule = 'test_regdelaybuffer'
jsonpath = '/workspaces/lab-4-behavioral-verilog-jasonwaseq/part2/regdelaybuffer'
jsonname = 'filelist.json'
root = '/workspaces/lab-4-behavioral-verilog-jasonwaseq'

    def runner(simulator, timescale, tbpath, params, defs=[], testname=None, pymodule=None, jsonpath=None, jsonname="filelist.json", root=None):
        """Run the simulator on test n, with parameters params, and defines
        defs. If n is none, it will run all tests"""
    
        # if json path is none, assume that it is the same as tbpath
        if(jsonpath is None):
            jsonpath = tbpath
    
        assert (os.path.exists(jsonpath)), "jsonpath directory must exist"
        top = get_top(jsonpath, jsonname)
    
        # if pymodule is none, assume that the python module name is test+<name of the top module>.
        if(pymodule is None):
            pymodule = "test_" + top
    
        if(testname is None):
            testdir = "all"
        else:
            testdir=testname
    
        # Assume all paths in the json file are relative to the repository root.
        if(root is None):
            root = git.Repo(search_parent_directories=True).working_tree_dir
    
        assert (os.path.exists(root)), "root directory path must exist"
    
        sources = get_sources(root, tbpath)
    
        work_dir = os.path.join(tbpath, "run", testdir, get_param_string(params), simulator)
        build_dir = os.path.join(tbpath, "build", get_param_string(params))
    
        # Icarus doesn't build, it just runs.
        if simulator.startswith("icarus"):
            build_dir = work_dir
    
        if simulator.startswith("verilator"):
            compile_args=["-Wno-fatal", "-DVM_TRACE_FST=1", "-DVM_TRACE=1"]
            plus_args = ["--trace", "--trace-fst"]
            if(not os.path.exists(work_dir)):
                os.makedirs(work_dir)
        else:
            compile_args=[]
            plus_args = []
    
>       run(verilog_sources=sources,
            simulator=simulator,
            toplevel=top,
            module=pymodule,
            compile_args=compile_args,
            plus_args=plus_args,
            sim_build=build_dir,
            timescale=timescale,
            parameters=params,
            defines=defs + ["VM_TRACE_FST=1", "VM_TRACE=1"],
            work_dir=work_dir,
            waves=True,
            testcase=testname)
E       SystemExit: FAILED 1 tests.

simulator = 'verilator', timescale = '1ps/1ps'
tbpath = '/workspaces/lab-4-behavioral-verilog-jasonwaseq/part2/regdelaybuffer'
params = {'delay_p': 2, 'width_p': 32}, defs = [], testname = 'in_fuzz_test'
pymodule = 'test_regdelaybuffer'
jsonpath = '/workspaces/lab-4-behavioral-verilog-jasonwaseq/part2/regdelaybuffer'
jsonname = 'filelist.json'
root = '/workspaces/lab-4-behavioral-verilog-jasonwaseq'

    def runner(simulator, timescale, tbpath, params, defs=[], testname=None, pymodule=None, jsonpath=None, jsonname="filelist.json", root=None):
        """Run the simulator on test n, with parameters params, and defines
        defs. If n is none, it will run all tests"""
    
        # if json path is none, assume that it is the same as tbpath
        if(jsonpath is None):
            jsonpath = tbpath
    
        assert (os.path.exists(jsonpath)), "jsonpath directory must exist"
        top = get_top(jsonpath, jsonname)
    
        # if pymodule is none, assume that the python module name is test+<name of the top module>.
        if(pymodule is None):
            pymodule = "test_" + top
    
        if(testname is None):
            testdir = "all"
        else:
            testdir=testname
    
        # Assume all paths in the json file are relative to the repository root.
        if(root is None):
            root = git.Repo(search_parent_directories=True).working_tree_dir
    
        assert (os.path.exists(root)), "root directory path must exist"
    
        sources = get_sources(root, tbpath)
    
        work_dir = os.path.join(tbpath, "run", testdir, get_param_string(params), simulator)
        build_dir = os.path.join(tbpath, "build", get_param_string(params))
    
        # Icarus doesn't build, it just runs.
        if simulator.startswith("icarus"):
            build_dir = work_dir
    
        if simulator.startswith("verilator"):
            compile_args=["-Wno-fatal", "-DVM_TRACE_FST=1", "-DVM_TRACE=1"]
            plus_args = ["--trace", "--trace-fst"]
            if(not os.path.exists(work_dir)):
                os.makedirs(work_dir)
        else:
            compile_args=[]
            plus_args = []
    
>       run(verilog_sources=sources,
            simulator=simulator,
            toplevel=top,
            module=pymodule,
            compile_args=compile_args,
            plus_args=plus_args,
            sim_build=build_dir,
            timescale=timescale,
            parameters=params,
            defines=defs + ["VM_TRACE_FST=1", "VM_TRACE=1"],
            work_dir=work_dir,
            waves=True,
            testcase=testname)
E       SystemExit: FAILED 1 tests.

simulator = 'verilator', timescale = '1ps/1ps'
tbpath = '/workspaces/lab-4-behavioral-verilog-jasonwaseq/part2/regdelaybuffer'
params = {'delay_p': 2, 'width_p': 7}, defs = [], testname = 'out_fuzz_test'
pymodule = 'test_regdelaybuffer'
jsonpath = '/workspaces/lab-4-behavioral-verilog-jasonwaseq/part2/regdelaybuffer'
jsonname = 'filelist.json'
root = '/workspaces/lab-4-behavioral-verilog-jasonwaseq'

    def runner(simulator, timescale, tbpath, params, defs=[], testname=None, pymodule=None, jsonpath=None, jsonname="filelist.json", root=None):
        """Run the simulator on test n, with parameters params, and defines
        defs. If n is none, it will run all tests"""
    
        # if json path is none, assume that it is the same as tbpath
        if(jsonpath is None):
            jsonpath = tbpath
    
        assert (os.path.exists(jsonpath)), "jsonpath directory must exist"
        top = get_top(jsonpath, jsonname)
    
        # if pymodule is none, assume that the python module name is test+<name of the top module>.
        if(pymodule is None):
            pymodule = "test_" + top
    
        if(testname is None):
            testdir = "all"
        else:
            testdir=testname
    
        # Assume all paths in the json file are relative to the repository root.
        if(root is None):
            root = git.Repo(search_parent_directories=True).working_tree_dir
    
        assert (os.path.exists(root)), "root directory path must exist"
    
        sources = get_sources(root, tbpath)
    
        work_dir = os.path.join(tbpath, "run", testdir, get_param_string(params), simulator)
        build_dir = os.path.join(tbpath, "build", get_param_string(params))
    
        # Icarus doesn't build, it just runs.
        if simulator.startswith("icarus"):
            build_dir = work_dir
    
        if simulator.startswith("verilator"):
            compile_args=["-Wno-fatal", "-DVM_TRACE_FST=1", "-DVM_TRACE=1"]
            plus_args = ["--trace", "--trace-fst"]
            if(not os.path.exists(work_dir)):
                os.makedirs(work_dir)
        else:
            compile_args=[]
            plus_args = []
    
>       run(verilog_sources=sources,
            simulator=simulator,
            toplevel=top,
            module=pymodule,
            compile_args=compile_args,
            plus_args=plus_args,
            sim_build=build_dir,
            timescale=timescale,
            parameters=params,
            defines=defs + ["VM_TRACE_FST=1", "VM_TRACE=1"],
            work_dir=work_dir,
            waves=True,
            testcase=testname)
E       SystemExit: FAILED 1 tests.

simulator = 'verilator', timescale = '1ps/1ps'
tbpath = '/workspaces/lab-4-behavioral-verilog-jasonwaseq/part2/regdelaybuffer'
params = {'delay_p': 4, 'width_p': 32}, defs = [], testname = 'full_bw_test'
pymodule = 'test_regdelaybuffer'
jsonpath = '/workspaces/lab-4-behavioral-verilog-jasonwaseq/part2/regdelaybuffer'
jsonname = 'filelist.json'
root = '/workspaces/lab-4-behavioral-verilog-jasonwaseq'

    def runner(simulator, timescale, tbpath, params, defs=[], testname=None, pymodule=None, jsonpath=None, jsonname="filelist.json", root=None):
        """Run the simulator on test n, with parameters params, and defines
        defs. If n is none, it will run all tests"""
    
        # if json path is none, assume that it is the same as tbpath
        if(jsonpath is None):
            jsonpath = tbpath
    
        assert (os.path.exists(jsonpath)), "jsonpath directory must exist"
        top = get_top(jsonpath, jsonname)
    
        # if pymodule is none, assume that the python module name is test+<name of the top module>.
        if(pymodule is None):
            pymodule = "test_" + top
    
        if(testname is None):
            testdir = "all"
        else:
            testdir=testname
    
        # Assume all paths in the json file are relative to the repository root.
        if(root is None):
            root = git.Repo(search_parent_directories=True).working_tree_dir
    
        assert (os.path.exists(root)), "root directory path must exist"
    
        sources = get_sources(root, tbpath)
    
        work_dir = os.path.join(tbpath, "run", testdir, get_param_string(params), simulator)
        build_dir = os.path.join(tbpath, "build", get_param_string(params))
    
        # Icarus doesn't build, it just runs.
        if simulator.startswith("icarus"):
            build_dir = work_dir
    
        if simulator.startswith("verilator"):
            compile_args=["-Wno-fatal", "-DVM_TRACE_FST=1", "-DVM_TRACE=1"]
            plus_args = ["--trace", "--trace-fst"]
            if(not os.path.exists(work_dir)):
                os.makedirs(work_dir)
        else:
            compile_args=[]
            plus_args = []
    
>       run(verilog_sources=sources,
            simulator=simulator,
            toplevel=top,
            module=pymodule,
            compile_args=compile_args,
            plus_args=plus_args,
            sim_build=build_dir,
            timescale=timescale,
            parameters=params,
            defines=defs + ["VM_TRACE_FST=1", "VM_TRACE=1"],
            work_dir=work_dir,
            waves=True,
            testcase=testname)
E       SystemExit: FAILED 1 tests.

    def runner(simulator, timescale, tbpath, params, defs=[], testname=None, pymodule=None, jsonpath=None, jsonname="filelist.json", root=None):
        """Run the simulator on test n, with parameters params, and defines
        defs. If n is none, it will run all tests"""
    
        # if json path is none, assume that it is the same as tbpath
        if(jsonpath is None):
            jsonpath = tbpath
    
        assert (os.path.exists(jsonpath)), "jsonpath directory must exist"
        top = get_top(jsonpath, jsonname)
    
        # if pymodule is none, assume that the python module name is test+<name of the top module>.
        if(pymodule is None):
            pymodule = "test_" + top
    
        if(testname is None):
            testdir = "all"
        else:
            testdir=testname
    
        # Assume all paths in the json file are relative to the repository root.
        if(root is None):
            root = git.Repo(search_parent_directories=True).working_tree_dir
    
        assert (os.path.exists(root)), "root directory path must exist"
    
        sources = get_sources(root, tbpath)
    
        work_dir = os.path.join(tbpath, "run", testdir, get_param_string(params), simulator)
        build_dir = os.path.join(tbpath, "build", get_param_string(params))
    
        # Icarus doesn't build, it just runs.
        if simulator.startswith("icarus"):
            build_dir = work_dir
    
        if simulator.startswith("verilator"):
            compile_args=["-Wno-fatal", "-DVM_TRACE_FST=1", "-DVM_TRACE=1"]
            plus_args = ["--trace", "--trace-fst"]
            if(not os.path.exists(work_dir)):
                os.makedirs(work_dir)
        else:
            compile_args=[]
            plus_args = []
    
>       run(verilog_sources=sources,
            simulator=simulator,
            toplevel=top,
            module=pymodule,
            compile_args=compile_args,
            plus_args=plus_args,
            sim_build=build_dir,
            timescale=timescale,
            parameters=params,
            defines=defs + ["VM_TRACE_FST=1", "VM_TRACE=1"],
            work_dir=work_dir,
            waves=True,
            testcase=testname)

simulator = 'icarus', timescale = '1ps/1ps'
tbpath = '/workspaces/lab-4-behavioral-verilog-jasonwaseq/part2/regdelaybuffer'
params = {'delay_p': 2, 'width_p': 7}, defs = [], testname = 'inout_fuzz_test'
pymodule = 'test_regdelaybuffer'
jsonpath = '/workspaces/lab-4-behavioral-verilog-jasonwaseq/part2/regdelaybuffer'
jsonname = 'filelist.json'
root = '/workspaces/lab-4-behavioral-verilog-jasonwaseq'

    def runner(simulator, timescale, tbpath, params, defs=[], testname=None, pymodule=None, jsonpath=None, jsonname="filelist.json", root=None):
        """Run the simulator on test n, with parameters params, and defines
        defs. If n is none, it will run all tests"""
    
        # if json path is none, assume that it is the same as tbpath
        if(jsonpath is None):
            jsonpath = tbpath
    
        assert (os.path.exists(jsonpath)), "jsonpath directory must exist"
        top = get_top(jsonpath, jsonname)
    
        # if pymodule is none, assume that the python module name is test+<name of the top module>.
        if(pymodule is None):
            pymodule = "test_" + top
    
        if(testname is None):
            testdir = "all"
        else:
            testdir=testname
    
        # Assume all paths in the json file are relative to the repository root.
        if(root is None):
            root = git.Repo(search_parent_directories=True).working_tree_dir
    
        assert (os.path.exists(root)), "root directory path must exist"
    
        sources = get_sources(root, tbpath)
    
        work_dir = os.path.join(tbpath, "run", testdir, get_param_string(params), simulator)
        build_dir = os.path.join(tbpath, "build", get_param_string(params))
    
        # Icarus doesn't build, it just runs.
        if simulator.startswith("icarus"):
            build_dir = work_dir
    
        if simulator.startswith("verilator"):
            compile_args=["-Wno-fatal", "-DVM_TRACE_FST=1", "-DVM_TRACE=1"]
            plus_args = ["--trace", "--trace-fst"]
            if(not os.path.exists(work_dir)):
                os.makedirs(work_dir)
        else:
            compile_args=[]
            plus_args = []
    
>       run(verilog_sources=sources,
            simulator=simulator,
            toplevel=top,
            module=pymodule,
            compile_args=compile_args,
            plus_args=plus_args,
            sim_build=build_dir,
            timescale=timescale,
            parameters=params,
            defines=defs + ["VM_TRACE_FST=1", "VM_TRACE=1"],
            work_dir=work_dir,
            waves=True,
            testcase=testname)
E       SystemExit: FAILED 1 tests.

    def runner(simulator, timescale, tbpath, params, defs=[], testname=None, pymodule=None, jsonpath=None, jsonname="filelist.json", root=None):
        """Run the simulator on test n, with parameters params, and defines
        defs. If n is none, it will run all tests"""
    
        # if json path is none, assume that it is the same as tbpath
        if(jsonpath is None):
            jsonpath = tbpath
    
        assert (os.path.exists(jsonpath)), "jsonpath directory must exist"
        top = get_top(jsonpath, jsonname)
    
        # if pymodule is none, assume that the python module name is test+<name of the top module>.
        if(pymodule is None):
            pymodule = "test_" + top
    
        if(testname is None):
            testdir = "all"
        else:
            testdir=testname
    
        # Assume all paths in the json file are relative to the repository root.
        if(root is None):
            root = git.Repo(search_parent_directories=True).working_tree_dir
    
        assert (os.path.exists(root)), "root directory path must exist"
    
        sources = get_sources(root, tbpath)
    
        work_dir = os.path.join(tbpath, "run", testdir, get_param_string(params), simulator)
        build_dir = os.path.join(tbpath, "build", get_param_string(params))
    
        # Icarus doesn't build, it just runs.
        if simulator.startswith("icarus"):
            build_dir = work_dir
    
        if simulator.startswith("verilator"):
            compile_args=["-Wno-fatal", "-DVM_TRACE_FST=1", "-DVM_TRACE=1"]
            plus_args = ["--trace", "--trace-fst"]
            if(not os.path.exists(work_dir)):
                os.makedirs(work_dir)
        else:
            compile_args=[]
            plus_args = []
    
>       run(verilog_sources=sources,
            simulator=simulator,
            toplevel=top,
            module=pymodule,
            compile_args=compile_args,
            plus_args=plus_args,
            sim_build=build_dir,
            timescale=timescale,
            parameters=params,
            defines=defs + ["VM_TRACE_FST=1", "VM_TRACE=1"],
            work_dir=work_dir,
            waves=True,
            testcase=testname)

_ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ 

simulator = 'icarus', timescale = '1ps/1ps'
tbpath = '/workspaces/lab-4-behavioral-verilog-jasonwaseq/part2/regdelaybuffer'
params = {'delay_p': 2, 'width_p': 7}, defs = [], testname = 'out_fuzz_test'
pymodule = 'test_regdelaybuffer'
jsonpath = '/workspaces/lab-4-behavioral-verilog-jasonwaseq/part2/regdelaybuffer'
jsonname = 'filelist.json'
root = '/workspaces/lab-4-behavioral-verilog-jasonwaseq'

    def runner(simulator, timescale, tbpath, params, defs=[], testname=None, pymodule=None, jsonpath=None, jsonname="filelist.json", root=None):
        """Run the simulator on test n, with parameters params, and defines
        defs. If n is none, it will run all tests"""
    
        # if json path is none, assume that it is the same as tbpath
        if(jsonpath is None):
            jsonpath = tbpath
    
        assert (os.path.exists(jsonpath)), "jsonpath directory must exist"
        top = get_top(jsonpath, jsonname)
    
        # if pymodule is none, assume that the python module name is test+<name of the top module>.
        if(pymodule is None):
            pymodule = "test_" + top
    
        if(testname is None):
            testdir = "all"
        else:
            testdir=testname
    
        # Assume all paths in the json file are relative to the repository root.
        if(root is None):
            root = git.Repo(search_parent_directories=True).working_tree_dir
    
        assert (os.path.exists(root)), "root directory path must exist"
    
        sources = get_sources(root, tbpath)
    
        work_dir = os.path.join(tbpath, "run", testdir, get_param_string(params), simulator)
        build_dir = os.path.join(tbpath, "build", get_param_string(params))
    
        # Icarus doesn't build, it just runs.
        if simulator.startswith("icarus"):
            build_dir = work_dir
    
        if simulator.startswith("verilator"):
            compile_args=["-Wno-fatal", "-DVM_TRACE_FST=1", "-DVM_TRACE=1"]
            plus_args = ["--trace", "--trace-fst"]
            if(not os.path.exists(work_dir)):
                os.makedirs(work_dir)
        else:
            compile_args=[]
            plus_args = []
    
>       run(verilog_sources=sources,
            simulator=simulator,
            toplevel=top,
            module=pymodule,
            compile_args=compile_args,
            plus_args=plus_args,
            sim_build=build_dir,
            timescale=timescale,
            parameters=params,
            defines=defs + ["VM_TRACE_FST=1", "VM_TRACE=1"],
            work_dir=work_dir,
            waves=True,
            testcase=testname)
E       SystemExit: FAILED 1 tests.

_ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ 

simulator = 'icarus', timescale = '1ps/1ps'
tbpath = '/workspaces/lab-4-behavioral-verilog-jasonwaseq/part2/regdelaybuffer'
params = {'delay_p': 4, 'width_p': 32}, defs = [], testname = 'full_bw_test'
pymodule = 'test_regdelaybuffer'
jsonpath = '/workspaces/lab-4-behavioral-verilog-jasonwaseq/part2/regdelaybuffer'
jsonname = 'filelist.json'
root = '/workspaces/lab-4-behavioral-verilog-jasonwaseq'

    def runner(simulator, timescale, tbpath, params, defs=[], testname=None, pymodule=None, jsonpath=None, jsonname="filelist.json", root=None):
        """Run the simulator on test n, with parameters params, and defines
        defs. If n is none, it will run all tests"""
    
        # if json path is none, assume that it is the same as tbpath
        if(jsonpath is None):
            jsonpath = tbpath
    
        assert (os.path.exists(jsonpath)), "jsonpath directory must exist"
        top = get_top(jsonpath, jsonname)
    
        # if pymodule is none, assume that the python module name is test+<name of the top module>.
        if(pymodule is None):
            pymodule = "test_" + top
    
        if(testname is None):
            testdir = "all"
        else:
            testdir=testname
    
        # Assume all paths in the json file are relative to the repository root.
        if(root is None):
            root = git.Repo(search_parent_directories=True).working_tree_dir
    
        assert (os.path.exists(root)), "root directory path must exist"
    
        sources = get_sources(root, tbpath)
    
        work_dir = os.path.join(tbpath, "run", testdir, get_param_string(params), simulator)
        build_dir = os.path.join(tbpath, "build", get_param_string(params))
    
        # Icarus doesn't build, it just runs.
        if simulator.startswith("icarus"):
            build_dir = work_dir
    
        if simulator.startswith("verilator"):
            compile_args=["-Wno-fatal", "-DVM_TRACE_FST=1", "-DVM_TRACE=1"]
            plus_args = ["--trace", "--trace-fst"]
            if(not os.path.exists(work_dir)):
                os.makedirs(work_dir)
        else:
            compile_args=[]
            plus_args = []
    
>       run(verilog_sources=sources,
            simulator=simulator,
            toplevel=top,
            module=pymodule,
            compile_args=compile_args,
            plus_args=plus_args,
            sim_build=build_dir,
            timescale=timescale,
            parameters=params,
            defines=defs + ["VM_TRACE_FST=1", "VM_TRACE=1"],
            work_dir=work_dir,
            waves=True,
            testcase=testname)
E       SystemExit: FAILED 1 tests.

    def runner(simulator, timescale, tbpath, params, defs=[], testname=None, pymodule=None, jsonpath=None, jsonname="filelist.json", root=None):
        """Run the simulator on test n, with parameters params, and defines
        defs. If n is none, it will run all tests"""
    
        # if json path is none, assume that it is the same as tbpath
        if(jsonpath is None):
            jsonpath = tbpath
    
        assert (os.path.exists(jsonpath)), "jsonpath directory must exist"
        top = get_top(jsonpath, jsonname)
    
        # if pymodule is none, assume that the python module name is test+<name of the top module>.
        if(pymodule is None):
            pymodule = "test_" + top
    
        if(testname is None):
            testdir = "all"
        else:
            testdir=testname
    
        # Assume all paths in the json file are relative to the repository root.
        if(root is None):
            root = git.Repo(search_parent_directories=True).working_tree_dir
    
        assert (os.path.exists(root)), "root directory path must exist"
    
        sources = get_sources(root, tbpath)
    
        work_dir = os.path.join(tbpath, "run", testdir, get_param_string(params), simulator)
        build_dir = os.path.join(tbpath, "build", get_param_string(params))
    
        # Icarus doesn't build, it just runs.
        if simulator.startswith("icarus"):
            build_dir = work_dir
    
        if simulator.startswith("verilator"):
            compile_args=["-Wno-fatal", "-DVM_TRACE_FST=1", "-DVM_TRACE=1"]
            plus_args = ["--trace", "--trace-fst"]
            if(not os.path.exists(work_dir)):
                os.makedirs(work_dir)
        else:
            compile_args=[]
            plus_args = []

    def runner(simulator, timescale, tbpath, params, defs=[], testname=None, pymodule=None, jsonpath=None, jsonname="filelist.json", root=None):
        """Run the simulator on test n, with parameters params, and defines
        defs. If n is none, it will run all tests"""
    
        # if json path is none, assume that it is the same as tbpath
        if(jsonpath is None):
            jsonpath = tbpath
    
        assert (os.path.exists(jsonpath)), "jsonpath directory must exist"
        top = get_top(jsonpath, jsonname)
    
        # if pymodule is none, assume that the python module name is test+<name of the top module>.
        if(pymodule is None):
            pymodule = "test_" + top
    
        if(testname is None):
            testdir = "all"
        else:
            testdir=testname
    
        # Assume all paths in the json file are relative to the repository root.
        if(root is None):
            root = git.Repo(search_parent_directories=True).working_tree_dir
    
        assert (os.path.exists(root)), "root directory path must exist"
    
        sources = get_sources(root, tbpath)
    
        work_dir = os.path.join(tbpath, "run", testdir, get_param_string(params), simulator)
        build_dir = os.path.join(tbpath, "build", get_param_string(params))
    
        # Icarus doesn't build, it just runs.
        if simulator.startswith("icarus"):
            build_dir = work_dir
    
        if simulator.startswith("verilator"):
            compile_args=["-Wno-fatal", "-DVM_TRACE_FST=1", "-DVM_TRACE=1"]
            plus_args = ["--trace", "--trace-fst"]
            if(not os.path.exists(work_dir)):
                os.makedirs(work_dir)
        else:
            compile_args=[]
            plus_args = []
    
>       run(verilog_sources=sources,
            simulator=simulator,
            toplevel=top,
            module=pymodule,

            timescale=timescale,
            parameters=params,
            defines=defs + ["VM_TRACE_FST=1", "VM_TRACE=1"],
            work_dir=work_dir,

    def runner(simulator, timescale, tbpath, params, defs=[], testname=None, pymodule=None, jsonpath=None, jsonname="filelist.json", root=None):
        """Run the simulator on test n, with parameters params, and defines
        defs. If n is none, it will run all tests"""
    
        # if json path is none, assume that it is the same as tbpath
        if(jsonpath is None):
            jsonpath = tbpath
    
        assert (os.path.exists(jsonpath)), "jsonpath directory must exist"
        top = get_top(jsonpath, jsonname)
    
        # if pymodule is none, assume that the python module name is test+<name of the top module>.
        if(pymodule is None):
            pymodule = "test_" + top
    
        if(testname is None):
            testdir = "all"
        else:
            testdir=testname
    
        # Assume all paths in the json file are relative to the repository root.
        if(root is None):
            root = git.Repo(search_parent_directories=True).working_tree_dir
    
        assert (os.path.exists(root)), "root directory path must exist"
    
        sources = get_sources(root, tbpath)
    
        work_dir = os.path.join(tbpath, "run", testdir, get_param_string(params), simulator)
        build_dir = os.path.join(tbpath, "build", get_param_string(params))
    
        # Icarus doesn't build, it just runs.
        if simulator.startswith("icarus"):
            build_dir = work_dir
    
        if simulator.startswith("verilator"):
            compile_args=["-Wno-fatal", "-DVM_TRACE_FST=1", "-DVM_TRACE=1"]
            plus_args = ["--trace", "--trace-fst"]
            if(not os.path.exists(work_dir)):
                os.makedirs(work_dir)
        else:
            compile_args=[]
            plus_args = []
    
>       run(verilog_sources=sources,
            simulator=simulator,
            toplevel=top,
            module=pymodule,
            compile_args=compile_args,
            plus_args=plus_args,
            sim_build=build_dir,
            timescale=timescale,
            parameters=params,
            defines=defs + ["VM_TRACE_FST=1", "VM_TRACE=1"],
            work_dir=work_dir,
            waves=True,
            testcase=testname)

    def runner(simulator, timescale, tbpath, params, defs=[], testname=None, pymodule=None, jsonpath=None, jsonname="filelist.json", root=None):
        """Run the simulator on test n, with parameters params, and defines
        defs. If n is none, it will run all tests"""
    
        # if json path is none, assume that it is the same as tbpath
        if(jsonpath is None):
            jsonpath = tbpath
    
        assert (os.path.exists(jsonpath)), "jsonpath directory must exist"
        top = get_top(jsonpath, jsonname)
    
        # if pymodule is none, assume that the python module name is test+<name of the top module>.
        if(pymodule is None):
            pymodule = "test_" + top
    
        if(testname is None):
            testdir = "all"
        else:
            testdir=testname
    
        # Assume all paths in the json file are relative to the repository root.
        if(root is None):
            root = git.Repo(search_parent_directories=True).working_tree_dir
    
        assert (os.path.exists(root)), "root directory path must exist"
    
        sources = get_sources(root, tbpath)
    
        work_dir = os.path.join(tbpath, "run", testdir, get_param_string(params), simulator)
        build_dir = os.path.join(tbpath, "build", get_param_string(params))
    
        # Icarus doesn't build, it just runs.
        if simulator.startswith("icarus"):
            build_dir = work_dir
    
        if simulator.startswith("verilator"):
            compile_args=["-Wno-fatal", "-DVM_TRACE_FST=1", "-DVM_TRACE=1"]
            plus_args = ["--trace", "--trace-fst"]
            if(not os.path.exists(work_dir)):
                os.makedirs(work_dir)
        else:
            compile_args=[]
            plus_args = []
    
>       run(verilog_sources=sources,
            simulator=simulator,
            toplevel=top,
            module=pymodule,
            compile_args=compile_args,
            plus_args=plus_args,
            sim_build=build_dir,
            timescale=timescale,
            parameters=params,
            defines=defs + ["VM_TRACE_FST=1", "VM_TRACE=1"],
            work_dir=work_dir,
            waves=True,
            testcase=testname)

    def runner(simulator, timescale, tbpath, params, defs=[], testname=None, pymodule=None, jsonpath=None, jsonname="filelist.json", root=None):
        """Run the simulator on test n, with parameters params, and defines
        defs. If n is none, it will run all tests"""
    
        # if json path is none, assume that it is the same as tbpath
        if(jsonpath is None):
            jsonpath = tbpath
    
        assert (os.path.exists(jsonpath)), "jsonpath directory must exist"
        top = get_top(jsonpath, jsonname)
    
        # if pymodule is none, assume that the python module name is test+<name of the top module>.
        if(pymodule is None):
            pymodule = "test_" + top
    
        if(testname is None):
            testdir = "all"
        else:
            testdir=testname
    
        # Assume all paths in the json file are relative to the repository root.
        if(root is None):
            root = git.Repo(search_parent_directories=True).working_tree_dir
    
        assert (os.path.exists(root)), "root directory path must exist"
    
        sources = get_sources(root, tbpath)
    
        work_dir = os.path.join(tbpath, "run", testdir, get_param_string(params), simulator)
        build_dir = os.path.join(tbpath, "build", get_param_string(params))
    
        # Icarus doesn't build, it just runs.
        if simulator.startswith("icarus"):
            build_dir = work_dir
    
        if simulator.startswith("verilator"):
            compile_args=["-Wno-fatal", "-DVM_TRACE_FST=1", "-DVM_TRACE=1"]
            plus_args = ["--trace", "--trace-fst"]
            if(not os.path.exists(work_dir)):
                os.makedirs(work_dir)
        else:
            compile_args=[]
            plus_args = []
    
>       run(verilog_sources=sources,
            simulator=simulator,
            toplevel=top,
            module=pymodule,
            compile_args=compile_args,
            plus_args=plus_args,
            sim_build=build_dir,
            timescale=timescale,
            parameters=params,
            defines=defs + ["VM_TRACE_FST=1", "VM_TRACE=1"],
            work_dir=work_dir,
            waves=True,
            testcase=testname)
